  <script>
    
    function loadYoutubeIframeAPI() {
      if(!document.getElementById('youtube_iframe_api')) {
        const tag = document.createElement('script')
        tag.id = 'youtube_iframe_api'
        tag.src = 'https://www.youtube.com/iframe_api'
        const firstScriptTag = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]
        firstScriptTag.parentNode.insertBefore(tag, firstScriptTag)
      }
    }
    function onYouTubeIframeAPIReady () {
      const youtubePlayers = document.querySelectorAll('[data-autoplay="true"][data-youtube-id]')
      if (youtubePlayers) {
        youtubePlayers.forEach(function (player) {
          new YT.Player(player, {
            events: {
              onReady: function (e) {
                e.target.playVideo()
              }
            }
          })
        })
      }
    }
  </script>

function prev(el, selector) {
  if (selector) {
    const prev = el.previousElementSibling;
    if (prev && prev.matches(selector)) {
      return prev;
    }
    return undefined;
  } else {
    return el.previousElementSibling;
  }
}
function next(el, selector) {
  if (selector) {
    const next = el.nextElementSibling;
    if (next && next.matches(selector)) {
      return next;
    }
    return undefined;
  } else {
    return el.nextElementSibling;
  }
}

var collectionPagination = function(){
    let categoryTitle = document.querySelector('.template-collection-banner h1').innerText;
    let prevText;
    let prevLink;
    
    if( prev([...document.querySelectorAll('#header__wrapper--md .header__navigation-dropdown-container a')].filter((el) => el.textContent.includes(categoryTitle))[0].parentNode) == undefined ){
      prevText = [...document.querySelectorAll('#header__wrapper--md .header__navigation-dropdown-container a')].filter((el) => el.textContent.includes(categoryTitle))[0].parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.querySelector('li:last-child').innerText;
      prevLink = [...document.querySelectorAll('#header__wrapper--md .header__navigation-dropdown-container a')].filter((el) => el.textContent.includes(categoryTitle))[0].parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.querySelector('li:last-child a').getAttribute("href");
    } else{
      prevText = prev([...document.querySelectorAll('#header__wrapper--md .header__navigation-dropdown-container a')].filter((el) => el.textContent.includes(categoryTitle))[0].parentNode).innerText;
      prevLink = prev([...document.querySelectorAll('#header__wrapper--md .header__navigation-dropdown-container a')].filter((el) => el.textContent.includes(categoryTitle))[0].parentNode).querySelector('a').getAttribute("href");
    }
    let nextText;
    let nextLink;
    if( next([...document.querySelectorAll('#header__wrapper--md .header__navigation-dropdown-container a')].filter((el) => el.textContent.includes(categoryTitle))[0].parentNode) == undefined ){
      console.log('got it from first item');
      nextText = [...document.querySelectorAll('#header__wrapper--md .header__navigation-dropdown-container a')].filter((el) => el.textContent.includes(categoryTitle))[0].parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.querySelector('li:first-child').innerText;
      nextLink = [...document.querySelectorAll('#header__wrapper--md .header__navigation-dropdown-container a')].filter((el) => el.textContent.includes(categoryTitle))[0].parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.querySelector('li:first-child a').getAttribute("href");
    } else {
      nextText = next([...document.querySelectorAll('#header__wrapper--md .header__navigation-dropdown-container a')].filter((el) => el.textContent.includes(categoryTitle))[0].parentNode).innerText;
      nextLink = next([...document.querySelectorAll('#header__wrapper--md .header__navigation-dropdown-container a')].filter((el) => el.textContent.includes(categoryTitle))[0].parentNode).querySelector('a').getAttribute("href");
    }
    let paginationHTML = `<div class="cat-footer-links">
       <a class="left" href="${prevLink}">${prevText}</a>
       <a class="right" href="${nextLink}">${nextText}</a>
     </div>`
     document.querySelector('.collection-section').innerHTML = document.querySelector('.collection-section').innerHTML + paginationHTML;
};

collectionPagination();

</script>

<!-- END sections: background-group --><script>
addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", (event) => {
function targetBlank() {
  // remove subdomain of current site's url and setup regex
  var internal = location.host.replace("www.", "");
      internal = new RegExp(internal, "i");
var el = document.querySelector('footer');      
  var a = el.getElementsByTagName('a'); // then, grab every link on the page
  for (var i = 0; i < a.length; i++) {
    var href = a[i].host; // set the host of each link
    if( !internal.test(href) ) { // make sure the href doesn't contain current site's host
      a[i].setAttribute('target', '_blank'); // if it doesn't, set attributes
    }
  }
};

// Run the function targetBlank()

targetBlank();
});
</script>

<script>
// adding alt tag for twitter analytics
document.addEventListener("DOMNodeInserted", function (event) {
  var newElement = event.target;
  if (newElement.src && (newElement.src.includes("https://analytics.twitter.com") || newElement.src.includes("https://t.co")) && !newElement.alt) {
    newElement.alt = "Twitter analytics";
  }
});
</script>

<script>
  // make footer menus collapsible on mobile
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    const navHeaders = document.querySelectorAll(".site-footer .navigation-heading-container");
    navHeaders.forEach(function (navHeader) {
      const navWrapper = navHeader.closest(".footer__griditem--navigation");
      const navContainer = navHeader.closest(".navigation-container");
      const navMenu = navContainer.querySelector(".nav-wrapper");

      if (navWrapper && navContainer && navMenu) {
        const navTitle = navHeader.textContent.trim();
        navWrapper.classList.add("collapsible", "collapsed");

        const navButton = document.createElement("button");
        navButton.setAttribute("class", "navigation-heading-button py-sm-md text_display_md text-left c-text-content-base w-full flex justify-between items-center");
        navButton.setAttribute("type", "button");
        navButton.setAttribute("aria-label", `Open ${navTitle} menu`);
        navButton.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
        navButton.innerHTML += `${navTitle} <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512" class="icon icon--arrow icon--arrow--chevron h-[1em] w-[1em]" fill="currentColor"><path d="M432.6 209.3l-191.1 183.1C235.1 397.8 229.1 400 224 400s-11.97-2.219-16.59-6.688L15.41 209.3C5.814 200.2 5.502 184.1 14.69 175.4c9.125-9.625 24.38-9.938 33.91-.7187L224 342.8l175.4-168c9.5-9.219 24.78-8.906 33.91 .7187C442.5 184.1 442.2 200.2 432.6 209.3z"></path></svg>`;
        navContainer.insertBefore(navButton, navMenu);

        navButton.addEventListener("click", function () {
          if (navWrapper.classList.contains("collapsed")) {
            navWrapper.classList.remove("collapsed");
            navButton.setAttribute("aria-label", `Close ${navTitle} menu`);
            navButton.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");
          } else {
            navWrapper.classList.add("collapsed");
            navButton.setAttribute("aria-label", `Open ${navTitle} menu`);
            navButton.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
          }
        });
      }
    });
  });
</script>

<b>Additional privacy rights</b><br><br>
